This makes debugging production issues difficult because operators see raw storage errors (e.g., \"sql: no rows in result set\") without knowing which flag evaluation triggered the error.\n\n**Problem**: 5 storage error points across 4 methods lack context enrichment:\n- `GetFlag()` (3 locations): Flag lookup phase, no context\n- `GetEvaluationRollouts()` (1 location): Boolean rollout evaluation phase, no context\n- `GetEvaluationRules()` (1 location): Variant rules lookup phase, no context\n- `GetEvaluationDistributions()` (1 location): Variant distribution lookup phase, no context\n\n**Goal**: Wrap storage errors with evaluation context (namespace, flag, phase) to make error messages more informative without breaking existing error type detection.\n\n## Implementation Strategy\n\n### Phase 1: Create Error Wrapping Infrastructure\n\n**File to Create**: `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/error.go`\n\nCreate an `EvaluationError` struct type that:\n1. Implements the `error` interface with a descriptive message\n\nThe error message format will be:\n```\n[evaluation error] phase: <phase>, namespace: <namespace>, flag: <flag>, error: <underlying-error>\n```\n\nThis approach:\n- Preserves the original error for inspection via `errors.Unwrap()`\n- Allows callers to still use `errors.As()` to check for original error types\n- Adds semantic context about where in the evaluation the error occurred\n- Doesn't break existing error type detection\n\n### Phase 2: Wrap Storage Errors in Evaluation Code\n\nModify error returns at the 5 storage error points:\n\n#### In `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/evaluation.go`:\n\n1. **Lines 26-28** (Variant method - Implements the `error` interface with a descriptive message\n\nThe error message format will be:\n```\n[evaluation error] phase: <phase>, namespace: <namespace>, flag: <flag>, error: <underlying-error>\n```\n\nThis approach:\n- Preserves the original error for inspection via `errors.Unwrap()`\n- Allows callers to still use `errors.As()` to check for original error types\n- Adds semantic context about where in the evaluation the error occurred\n- Doesn't break existing error type detection\n\n### Phase 2: Wrap Storage Errors in Evaluation Code\n\nModify error returns at the 5 storage error points:\n\n#### In `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/evaluation.go`:\n\n1. **Lines 26-28** (Variant method - GetFlag):\n   ```go\n   flag, err := s.store.GetFlag(ctx, ...)\n   if err != nil {\n       return nil, WrapEvaluationError(err, r.NamespaceKey, r.FlagKey, \"flag_lookup\")\n   }\n   ```\n\n3. **Lines 132-135** (boolean method - This makes debugging production issues difficult because operators see raw storage errors (e.g., \"sql: no rows in result set\") without knowing which flag evaluation triggered the error.\n\n**Problem**: 5 storage error points across 4 methods lack context enrichment:\n- `GetFlag()` (3 locations): Flag lookup phase, no context\n- `GetEvaluationRollouts()` (1 location): Boolean rollout evaluation phase, no context\n- `GetEvaluationRules()` (1 location): Variant rules lookup phase, no context\n- `GetEvaluationDistributions()` (1 location): Variant distribution lookup phase, no context\n\n**Goal**: Wrap storage errors with evaluation context (namespace, flag, phase) to make error messages more informative without breaking existing error type detection.\n\n## Implementation Strategy\n\n### Phase 1: Create Error Wrapping Infrastructure\n\n**File to Create**: `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/error.go`\n\nCreate an `EvaluationError` struct type that:\n1. Implements the `error` interface with a descriptive message\n\nThe error message format will be:\n```\n[evaluation error] phase: <phase>, namespace: <namespace>, flag: <flag>, error: <underlying-error>\n```\n\nThis approach:\n- Preserves the original error for inspection via `errors.Unwrap()`\n- Allows callers to still use `errors.As()` to check for original error types\n- Adds semantic context about where in the evaluation the error occurred\n- Doesn't break existing error type detection\n\n### Phase 2: Wrap Storage Errors in Evaluation Code\n\nModify error returns at the 5 storage error points:\n\n#### In `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/evaluation.go`:\n\n1. **Lines 26-28** (Variant method - Implements the `error` interface with a descriptive message\n\nThe error message format will be:\n```\n[evaluation error] phase: <phase>, namespace: <namespace>, flag: <flag>, error: <underlying-error>\n```\n\nThis approach:\n- Preserves the original error for inspection via `errors.Unwrap()`\n- Allows callers to still use `errors.As()` to check for original error types\n- Adds semantic context about where in the evaluation the error occurred\n- Doesn't break existing error type detection\n\n### Phase 2: Wrap Storage Errors in Evaluation Code\n\nModify error returns at the 5 storage error points:\n\n#### In `/workspace/internal/server/evaluation/evaluation.go`:\n\n1. **Lines 26-28** (Variant method -
